< Text>
A wonderfully clean and friendly store!  I come here for my animals' needs and treats - dogs, rabbits, rats, tortoises and gecko!  The staff is very helpful and helped me find the perfect dog food when my little guy had medical issues.  They have a good variety of refrigerated food for dogs too!  I enjoy shopping here and look forward to each month when they host The Rabbit Haven team.  The bunnies are SO cute!  When you adopt a bunny there, the store gives you a generous discount on all your food and supplies - best prices for bags of Timothy/Orchard hay!

Keep up the great work, For Other Living Things Staff!!<//Text>

<text>**Update**
Since my last review I can only add to how impressed I am with service and quality of their water.  They also offer Alkaline water which is what I prefer.

My wife and I had a little girl since our last review and all through those trying months my wife and I were drinking this water.  After our baby was born, we had also used the water for not only our consumption, but also for making our little girl's bottles because of the water's purity.

Overall still the only water we drink and not only is it so much cheaper than buying bottle water but it tastes better and your purchasing from a wonderful family owned business.

*Original Post*
I've been going to Healthy Water for about two months now.  Family owned and how more polite, friendly, and helpful can they be?  I previously used a Brita then PUR filters with my tap water, but that only filtered out some of the particulates in the water.

Healthy water has a top of the line water filtration system that even removes the fluoride amongst many other unwanted contaminants that carbon filters cannot .  The owner explained to me that they perform consistent maintenance to keep their filtration system clean which I can't say for other water stores.  The purity is amazing and the price is right!

My wife who is now six months pregnant loves carbonated water so we use the water with a Soda Stream to make sure she always has the best carbonated water.  I'm writing this review because I am about to head on over and get a refill for my jug and right now I wouldn't be going any place else.  I will try out the alkaline to see if it's worth it.

Five stars.< /text>< Rate>

1512234940208<//date>
<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
This time at the Kyle's Kitchen I was pleasantly surprised with the very best Earth Burger I've ever had! I'm not one for something trying to mimic a hamburger. I'd rather taste vegetables and legumes. While I love to eat vegetarian I am not actually a vegetarian. Which says a whole lot for his Earth Burger. I don't know what his recipe for this is but it is awesome! I adore the toppings on this Earth Burger. There are crushed avocado, arugula, caramelized onion, organic sprouts, tomatoes and garlic aioli. The Earth burger patty itself is a little on the soft side. You have to expect that because it is garbanzo bean based I think. I found that when I thought of it as a filling instead of a burger somehow in my mind it was even better. I'm telling you if you want a vegetarian burger, this is great!< /Review>

< Review>
Bennett loves DeeDee. He hates water and runs away when I try give him a bath in my tub.  DeeDee takes so much time with him and makes him feel safe on that special drip stand -- to my surprise he doesn't complain in the bath. She makes sure the water is warm, talks to him and is gentle. She uses the blow dryer at first then switches to another quiet warmer thing for his face. Her brush doesn't hurt. She trims his nails with care and then files them. The bath includes a "privates" shave. He didn't need a haircut this time but she even trimmed around his face a little. I drive from West Hollywood to Silver Lake for his app't and wait to avoid two round trips. She is very accommodating and "we" appreciate her. I don't like going to a groomer that hides the process behind closed doors. I want to see where he is being bathed or kept waiting. I heard so many horror stories that I used to groom him myself (not nearly as well as she does)....I originally came here to use the "pet wash" (also very clean -- great towels and shampoos provided) -- but when I saw how she treated all the "fur clients", I began by having her just clip his nails. She took a lot of time with him (like most dogs, he didn't like it). Now, he knows she doesn't hurt him (and gives treats between paw clips :), so I decided to let her give him the Dee Dee Magic of a complete bath or when needed complete groom. I'm so happy to have found this. It is part of Urban Pet -- I've found that everyone who works here loves animals, is knowledgeable and very helpful. Bennett and his Mom say "Thank you Dee Dee".< /Review>

< text>
5 Stars for this poke joint!  Found this little poke shop by accident on yelp, called and asked if they were open then decided to stop by -- and we are so glad we did.  Fantastic service and food.  The woman who assisted us was incredibly nice and patient, considering this was our first visit.  She explained their process and offerings, and also made personal suggestions on which sauces pair well together.  By the way, the sesame oil is a game changer!!  Why haven't I had it before?  We each both had a small (2 scoops fish) and were very full and satisfied.  For like $2-3 you can turn your bowl into a combo and they have some interesting drink options.  New favorite place!

They are exercising proper COVID precautions and also do delivery.  Highly recommend!< /text>

<username>Pete Shieh<//username><time>1470259270935< /time><rating>4<//rating><review>Well, I have to say welcome to Cypress PokiDoki! I love Poke and this place being next to Costco (Ironically they recently offered it prepacked on weekends), would visit here for a healthy alternative anytime!

Their recent Grand Opening had FREE, yes FREE medium size Poke bowls ( reg. 8.50 for 3 items) in which you can pick your base from chips, salad, white rice, or brown rice. Then you pick your proteins from albacore, tuna, salmon, shrimp, scallops, eggs. The avocado and imo crabmeat is standard. Extra avo is $1 more. Then you pick your toppings. I just pick all cuz pretty much it's everything I want, including wasabi.  To finish, you pick your sauce. I have to say, I think this place is Korean owned and I'm a little disappointed in the sauce. It's not spicy at all in any way for the spicy version. The regular sauce just tasted like sweet soy sauce.

I noticed on the 2nd day they gave out less on the bowl. I'm not complaining, I'm still grateful to have tried your poke bowl for free and your pokinade which has chunks of strawberry and basil. I do wish the lemon sour intensity was more because it tasted a little watered down for me. But thank goodness you do offer sweet green tea next to the soda dispenser.

I do like the size of the fish chunks here, it's not big nor terribly small. Your servers were friendly with a smile so that in itself was sign for me to come back.

Oh yeah, the blurring loud music when I was there pretty much gave away that the owners were Korean.  If you ever been to those KBBQ places, you know what I'm talking about!</review><pics>None<//pics>< Resp>
None< /Resp>
